style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">2-2-2</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-top:12px;text-align:justify;text-indent:24px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">Miami, </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">March&#160;19, 2020</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">&#32;-- Lennar Corporation (NYSE: LEN and LEN.B)</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">,</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">one of</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">the nation&#8217;s leading homebuilders, today reported results for its </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">first quarter ended February 29, 2020</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">. </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">First quarter</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;net earnings attributable to Lennar in </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2020</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;were </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$398.5 million</font><font to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">first quarter</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;net earnings attributable to Lennar in </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2019</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$239.9 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$0.74</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;per diluted share.</font></div><div style="line-height:155%;padding-top:8px;text-align:justify;text-indent:24px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">Stuart Miller, Executive Chairman of Lennar, said, &#8220;Although today we are announcing our first quarter 2020 results, the events that have occurred since quarter-end currently command our focus and attention. With a near shutdown of large portions of our national economy, we are all stretching our minds to understand the parameters of the rapidly evolving landscape, while we contemplate what the future holds. Accordingly, our first quarter conference call this morning will be focused on Lennar&#8217;s oversight and management through the current crisis, and the steady-handed approach that we have applied.&#8221;</font></div><div style="line-height:155%;padding-top:8px;text-align:justify;text-indent:24px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">Mr. Miller continued, &#8220;First and foremost, our senior management team is evaluating every aspect of our company to determine how we protect the safety, health and hygiene of each and every one of our associates, customers and building partners, while we maintain our business. In that regard, we have engaged a distinguished medical professional, Dr. Pascal Goldschmidt, as our Chief Medical Officer who is assisting us in looking into every step of every business process to ensure we fully understand its impact on the health of every individual involved.</font></div><div style="line-height:155%;padding-top:8px;text-align:justify;text-indent:24px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#8220;Next, with safety, health and hygiene first, we are focused on the day to day operation of maintaining the parts of our business that are sustainable, while the national economy is struggling with a deepening pause, in order to &#8216;flatten the COVID-19 curve.&#8217; Like food from the grocer is essential, our customers need a safe and secure place called &#8216;home,&#8217; while the country moves from today&#8217;s landscape of uncertainty to knowing that &#8216;this too, shall pass.&#8217; Balancing people, safety and pause, with production and closings is difficult, and has the undivided focus of our entire seasoned and experienced management team.</font></div><div style="line-height:155%;padding-top:8px;text-align:justify;text-indent:24px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#8220;Third, we are managing every element of our balance sheet, cash management and cash flow. We are managing the inflow, and especially the outflow, of cash to maintain a strong foundation. Lennar&#8217;s liquidity and strong balance sheet remain a stabilizing factor in enabling our company to help absorb the shock that is moving through the economy at this time. We are well positioned for stability today, as well as for opportunity when markets settle.</font></div><div style="line-height:155%;padding-top:8px;text-align:justify;text-indent:24px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">Mr. Miller concluded, &#8220;As you can see in the schedules in our earnings release, our first quarter results achieved and exceeded all expected metrics and we had been on track to expand on our guidance for the year. We have been focused on reducing land spend and land holdings to grow cash flow and fortify our balance sheet. That strategy was well-timed and has positioned us well. In the context of today&#8217;s widespread shutdowns, we are choosing to suspend guidance as the world resets and finds its way forward. In the meantime, the laser focus of our experienced, hands-on management team will navigate, make necessary adjustments and guide Lennar through current market conditions.&#8221;</font></div><div style="line-height:155%;padding-top:8px;text-align:justify;text-indent:24px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div><br></div><hr style="line-height:120%;padding-top:12px;text-align:center;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">THREE MONTHS ENDED </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">FEBRUARY&#160;29, 2020</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">&#32;COMPARED TO </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">THREE MONTHS ENDED </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">FEBRUARY&#160;28, 2019</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:12px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;text-decoration:underline;">Homebuilding</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-top:12px;text-align:justify;text-indent:24px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">Revenues from home sales </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">increased</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">15%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">first quarter of 2020</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$4.1 billion</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;from </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$3.6 billion</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">first quarter of 2019</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">. Revenues were higher primarily due to a </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">17%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">increase</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the number of home deliveries, excluding unconsolidated entities, partially offset by a </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">2%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">decrease</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the average sales price of homes delivered. New home deliveries, excluding unconsolidated entities, </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">increased</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">10,313</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;homes in the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">first quarter of 2020</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;from </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">8,802</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;homes in the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">first quarter of 2019</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, as a result of an increase in home deliveries in all homebuilding segments. The average sales price of homes delivered was </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$402,000</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">first quarter of 2020</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, compared to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$410,000</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">first quarter of 2019</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">. The decrease in average sales price primarily resulted from continuing to shift to lower-priced communities.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-top:12px;text-align:justify;text-indent:24px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">Gross margin on home sales were </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$849.0 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">20.5%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, in the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">first quarter of 2020</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, compared to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$726.1 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">20.1%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">first quarter of 2019</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">. The gross margin percentage on home sales increased primarily due to the Company's focus on reducing construction costs.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-top:12px;text-align:justify;text-indent:24px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">Selling, general and administrative expenses were </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$378.9 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">first quarter of 2020</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, compared to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$343.3 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">first quarter of 2019</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">. As a percentage of revenues from home sales, selling, general and administrative expenses improved to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">9.2%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">first quarter of 2020</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, from </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">9.5%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">first quarter of 2019</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, due to improved operating leverage primarily as a result of an increase in home deliveries.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-top:12px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;text-decoration:underline;">Financial Services</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-top:12px;text-align:justify;text-indent:24px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">Operating earnings for the Financial Services segment were </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$58.2 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">first quarter of 2020</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;(which included </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$21.8 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">first quarter of 2019</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;(which included </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$19.0 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;of operating earnings and an add back of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$2.8 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;of net loss attributable to noncontrolling interests). Operating earnings increased due to an improvement in the mortgage business as a result of an increase in volume and margin, as well as reductions in loan origination costs driven in part by technology initiatives. Additionally, operating earnings of the Company's title business increased primarily due to an increase in volume. </font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-top:12px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;text-decoration:underline;">Other Ancillary Businesses</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-top:12px;text-align:justify;text-indent:24px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">Operating earnings for the Multifamily segment were $1.8 million in the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">first quarter of 2020</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;(which included $0.1 million of net earnings attributable to noncontrolling interests), compared to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$6.8 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">first quarter of 2019</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">. Operating earnings for the Lennar Other segment were </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$0.9 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">first quarter of 2020</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, compared to $3.1 million in the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">first quarter of 2019</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;(which included $0.1 million of net earnings attributable to noncontrolling interests). </font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-top:12px;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-top:12px;text-align:justify;text-indent:24px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">For the </font><font The Company's overall effective income tax rate was </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">7.5%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;for the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">three months ended February 29, 2020</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;and </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">24.9%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;for the three months ended </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">February&#160;28, 2019</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">. The reduction in the overall effective income tax rate is primarily due to the extension of the new energy efficient home tax credit during the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">first quarter of 2020</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-top:12px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;text-decoration:underline;">Share Repurchases</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-top:12px;text-align:justify;text-indent:24px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">During the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">first quarter of 2020</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, the Company repurchased a total 4.4 million shares of its common stock, including 4.3 million Class A shares and 0.1 million Class B shares, for $288.4 million at an average per share price of $66.42 per Class A share and $53.52 per Class B share.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-top:12px;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;text-decoration:underline;">Liquidity</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-top:12px;text-align:justify;text-indent:24px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">At </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">February&#160;29, 2020</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, the Company had </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$785.0 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;of Homebuilding cash &amp; cash equivalents. Also at </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">February&#160;29, 2020</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">, the Company had </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">$300.0 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#32;of outstanding borrowings under its revolving credit facility, thereby providing $2.1 billion of available capacity.</font></div><div><br></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div><a name="s71F2BB77BFD155EB919E833167566288"></a></div><div><br></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-top:12px;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">5-5-5</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">About Lennar</font></div><div style="line-height:150%;text-align:justify;text-indent:24px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">Lennar Corporation, founded in 1954, is one of the nation&#8217;s leading builders of quality homes for all generations. The Company builds affordable, move-up and active adult homes primarily under the Lennar brand name. Lennar&#8217;s Financial Services segment provides mortgage financing, title and closing services primarily for buyers of Lennar&#8217;s </font></div><div style="line-height:150%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">homes and, through LMF Commercial, originates mortgage loans secured primarily by commercial real estate properties throughout the United States. Lennar's Multifamily segment is a nationwide developer of high-quality multifamily rental properties. Lennar Ventures drives the Company's technology and innovation strategies. For more information about Lennar, please visit www.lennar.com.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;"><hr></div><div style="line-height:150%;text-align:justify;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">Note Regarding Forward-Looking Statements:</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">Some of the statements in this press release are "forward-looking statements," as that term is defined in the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995, including statements relating to the homebuilding market and other markets in which we participate. You can identify forward-looking statements by the fact that these statements do not relate strictly to historical or current matters. Rather, forward-looking statements relate to anticipated or expected events, activities, trends or results. Accordingly, these forward-looking statements should be evaluated with consideration given to the many risks and uncertainties inherent in our business that could cause actual results and events to differ materially from those anticipated by the forward-looking statements. Important factors that could cause such differences include&#160;the potential negative impact of the coronavirus (COVID-19) outbreak on our ability to continue our Homebuilding or Multifamily development activities at normal levels or at all in affected regions; the duration, impact and severity of the COVID-19 outbreak; slowdowns in real estate markets in regions where we have significant Homebuilding or Multifamily development activities; increases in operating costs, including costs related to construction materials, labor, real estate taxes and insurance, which exceed our ability to increase prices, both in our Homebuilding and Multifamily businesses; reduced availability of mortgage financing or increased interest rates; decreased demand for our homes or Multifamily rental properties, or our inability to successfully sell our apartment developments; natural disasters or catastrophic events for which our insurance may not provide adequate coverage; our ability to successfully execute our strategies, including our land lighter strategy; a decline in the value of the land and home inventories we maintain and resulting possible future writedowns of the carrying value of our real estate assets; unfavorable losses in legal proceedings; conditions in the capital, credit and financial markets; changes in laws, regulations or the regulatory environment affecting our business, and the risks described in our filings with the Securities and Exchange Commission, including our Form 10-K for the fiscal year ended November 30, 2019. non-GAAP financial measure defined as earnings before interest and taxes. This financial measure has been presented because the Company finds it important and useful in evaluating its performance and believes that it helps readers of the Company's financial statements compare its operations with those of its competitors. Although management finds EBIT to be an important measure in conducting and evaluating the Company's operations, this measure has limitations as an analytical tool as it is not reflective of the actual profitability generated by the Company during the period. Management compensates for the limitations of using EBIT by using this non-GAAP measure only to supplement the Company's GAAP results. Due to the limitations discussed, EBIT should not be viewed in isolation, as it is not a substitute for GAAP measures.</font></div></td></tr></table><div style="font-family:inherit;font-size:9pt;">(1)</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:top;padding-left:24px;"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:9pt;text-indent:-24px;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:9pt;">Net homebuilding debt to total capital is a non-GAAP financial measure defined as net homebuilding debt (homebuilding debt less homebuilding cash and cash equivalents) divided by total capital (net homebuilding debt plus stockholders' equity). The Company believes the ratio of net homebuilding debt to total capital is a relevant and a useful financial measure to investors in understanding the leverage employed in homebuilding operations. However, because net homebuilding debt to total capital is not calculated in accordance with GAAP, this financial measure should not be considered in isolation or as an alternative to financial measures prescribed by GAAP. Rather, this non-GAAP financial measure should be used to supplement the Company's GAAP results.</font></div></td></tr></table><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div><br></div><div style="text-align:center;"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div>	</div></body>
